   346|         1|  7.86781e-06|  7.86781e-06|  0.00%|    def calculate_dynamic_priority_rules(self,eligible,current_time,current_consumption, active_list,finish_times):
   347|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|        """
   348|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            Calculates IRSM, WCS, ACS priority values
   349|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|
   350|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            Parameters:
   351|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                eligible: eligible set of jobs based on both precedence and resource constraints
   352|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                current_time: Current time when priorities are being calculated
   353|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                current_consumption: Amount of resources being consumed currently
   354|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                active_list: List of jobs which are scheduled and currently active
   355|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                finish_times: Finish times of each job
   356|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|        """
   357|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|        for j in eligible:
   358|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            sum_e_vals=0 #Sum of E(i,j) over all i
   359|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            max_e_val=0 #Max of E(i,j) over all i
   360|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            irsm_val=0 # Max of max(0,E(j,i) -LS_i) over all i
   361|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|            for i in eligible:
   362|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                if(i!=j):
   363|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                    irsm_val=max(self.earliest_start(j,i,current_time,current_consumption,active_list,finish_times)-self.latest_start_times[i],irsm_val)
   364|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                    curr_e_val=self.earliest_start(i,j,current_time,current_consumption,active_list,finish_times)
   365|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                    max_e_val=max(curr_e_val,max_e_val)
   366|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                    sum_e_vals+=curr_e_val
